### [172] [CacheMPC: Certified Cached Model Predictive Control for Quadruped Locomotion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28300)
*Nimesh Khandelwal,Mehul Anand,Shakti S. Gupta,Mangal Kothari*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该论文提出了Certified CacheMPC，一种基于局部敏感哈希缓存的MPC方法，通过缓存接触力轨迹并验证可行性来加速四足机器人控制，在模拟中实现25倍速度提升，硬件上实现18.7倍提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统MPC在嵌入式处理器上每周期求解QP限制了更新频率，而四足运动步态会在有界状态空间内重复，使得MPC解可以缓存重用，从而提升计算效率。

Method: 提出Certified CacheMPC：使用局部敏感哈希缓存按接触模式分区的水平接触力轨迹，在查询时通过后验证书验证原始可行性和成本次优性的拉格朗日对偶间隙上界。采用有界预算控制器调度，结合top-K认证检索、截止时间限制的QP求解和上次认证回退策略。

Result: 在Unitree Go2机器人上进行了2038次冷控制器MuJoCo试验，包括600次n=50的边界测试。无门控缓存实现模拟中25倍中值求解时间加速，硬件上18.7倍加速。在n=50时，缓存变体与无缓存基线在闭环稳定率上无统计显著差异。

Conclusion: Certified CacheMPC能显著加速MPC求解而不影响控制性能，为四足机器人嵌入式控制提供了高效的缓存解决方案，但证书对闭环安全性的贡献在当前样本量下尚无法确定。

Abstract: Model Predictive Control (MPC) is the standard predictive layer in hierarchical quadruped controllers, but the per-cycle QP solve limits the update rate achievable on embedded processors. Because legged gaits revisit a bounded region of state space, MPC solutions admit caching and reuse. This paper proposes \emph{Certified CacheMPC}: a Locality-Sensitive-Hashed cache of horizon contact-force trajectories, partitioned by contact mode, retrieved at query time and accepted only when an a-posteriori per-query certificate confirms primal feasibility and a Lagrangian dual-gap upper bound on cost suboptimality. A bounded-budget controller schedule combines top-$K$ certified retrieval, a deadline-bounded QP solve, and a shifted last-certified fallback. The framework is evaluated on a Unitree Go2 across $2{,}038$ usable cold-controller MuJoCo trials, including a $600$-trial $n\!=\!50$ campaign at three failure-boundary cells, and a first-deploy session on the on-robot NVIDIA Orin NX. The un-gated cache delivers a $25\times$ median solve-time speedup in simulation and an $18.7\times$ median speedup on hardware. At $n\!=\!50$ no statistically significant difference in closed-loop stable rate is detected between the cache variants and the no-cache baseline at any tested cell. The certificate's contribution to closed-loop safety is not resolvable at the present sample size.

</details>


### [173] [WARP-RM: A Warp-Augmented Relative Progress Reward Model for Data Curation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28320)
*Justin Yu,Andrew Goldberg,Kavish Kondap,Karim El-Refai,Ethan Ransing,Qianzhong Chen,Mac Schwager,Fred Shentu,Philipp Wu,Ken Goldberg*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: WARP是一种完全自监督的算法，通过时间扭曲增强从成功演示中学习密集、有符号的相对进度幅度，然后利用这些进度估计在行为克隆中加权高优势动作块，显著提高了在混合质量数据集上的策略性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 模仿学习需要大规模数据集，但人类远程操作不可避免地产生包含犹豫和恢复的混合质量演示。现有的帧级进度奖励模型要么使用有标签噪声的绝对时间进度代理，要么需要昂贵的人工标注来定义子任务边界。

Method: 提出WARP算法：1) 通过时间扭曲增强（可变播放速度和反转）生成每帧进度目标；2) 训练WARP-RM预测输入帧之间的归一化经过时间；3) 聚合重叠窗口的预测得到密集帧级进度信号；4) 引入WARP-BC，利用标量奖励估计在行为克隆中加权高优势动作块，其中块级优势通过聚合每帧奖励获得。

Result: 在物理双臂机器人系统上评估，执行长视界可变形物体操作任务（从随机皱褶状态折叠T恤）。当训练数据集扩展到包含更多低效演示时，WARP-BC保持19/20的成功率，而普通BC下降到2/20，吞吐量提高了18倍。

Conclusion: WARP提供了一种完全自监督的方法，从成功演示中学习密集的相对进度信号，显著提高了在混合质量数据集上的模仿学习性能，特别是在长视界可变形物体操作任务中表现出色。

Abstract: Scaling imitation learning requires large datasets, yet human teleoperation inevitably produces mixed-quality demonstrations containing hesitations and recoveries. Prior frame-level progress reward models supervise on absolute temporal progress proxies that suffer from label noise, or require costly human annotations to define subtask boundaries. We present WARP (Warp-Augmented Relative Progress), a novel fully self-supervised algorithm for learning dense, signed relative progress magnitudes directly from successful demonstrations. WARP generates per-frame progress targets via time-warp augmentations of demonstrations (variable playback speeds and reversals) and we train WARP-RM to predict the normalized elapsed time between input frames. Aggregating these predictions across overlapping windows yields a dense frame-level progress signal. We then introduce WARP-BC, which leverages these scalar reward estimates to upweight high-advantage action chunks during behavior cloning, where chunk-level advantage is obtained by aggregating per-frame rewards. We evaluate our approach on a physical bimanual robot system performing a long-horizon deformable object manipulation task: folding T-shirts from a random crumpled start. To evaluate policy robustness against suboptimal data, we construct training datasets of varying quality using episode length as a proxy for teleoperation sub-optimality. As the dataset is widened to admit more inefficiencies, WARP-BC maintains a 19/20 success rate compared to vanilla BC's collapse to 2/20, improving throughput by up to 18x.

</details>


### [174] [DexCompose: Reusing Dexterous Policies for Multi-Task Manipulation with a Single Hand](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28323)
*Dihong Huang,Zhenyu Wei,Zhuxiu Xu,Yunchao Yao,Sikai Li,Mingyu Ding*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: DexCompose：一种基于角色感知的残差组合框架，通过明确的手指级动作所有权来复用预训练的灵巧策略，实现多任务操作


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的灵巧操作策略可以解决单个技能，但组合成多任务操作仍具挑战。在现有技能基础上添加新任务时，手指和接触模式会产生冲突需求，导致保持现有操作结果和执行新任务之间的破坏性干扰。

Method: DexCompose首先从第一个技能收集成功的任务后状态，并通过候选手指掩码进行释放测试，识别哪些手指对维持已建立的技能状态是必要的。然后训练两个非对称残差模块：一个有界的残差稳定器用于任务保持，另一个上下文感知残差仅在分配给新任务的动作子空间内适应冻结的下游策略。

Result: 在涵盖4个物体保持技能和4个下游交互的16个复合灵巧操作任务上，DexCompose实现了77.4%的平均复合成功率。

Conclusion: 具有双重残差的结构化动作所有权为超越传统策略链的灵巧技能组合提供了有前景的方向。

Abstract: Dexterous manipulation policies can solve individual skills, but composing them to perform multiple tasks with a single hand remains challenging. Adding a new task on top of an existing manipulation skill often imposes conflicting demands on overlapping fingers and contact modes, causing destructive interference between preserving an existing manipulation outcome and executing a new one. We propose DexCompose, a role-aware residual composition framework that reuses pretrained dexterous policies for multi-task manipulation through explicit finger-level action ownership. Given two pretrained full-hand policies, DexCompose first collects successful post-task states from the first skill and performs release tests over candidate finger masks to identify which fingers are necessary for maintaining the established skill state. It then trains two asymmetric residual modules: a bounded residual stabilizer for task preservation, and a context-aware residual that adapts the frozen downstream policy only within the action subspace assigned to the new task. We evaluate the framework on 16 composite dexterous manipulation tasks spanning four object-retention skills and four downstream interactions. DexCompose achieves a 77.4% average composite success rate, demonstrating that structural action ownership with dual residuals offers a promising direction for composing dexterous skills beyond conventional policy chaining.

</details>


### [175] [Support-Constrained RL Enables Real-World Policy Improvement without Real-World Experience](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27475)
*Raymond Yu,William Huey,Mustafa Mukadam,Anusha Nagabandi,Abhishek Gupta*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: SCORE是一个真实-仿真-真实框架，通过约束仿真中的强化学习到预训练生成策略的支持域，实现安全可转移的策略改进，在八项灵巧操作任务中将成功率从37.8%提升至89.9%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实世界训练的机器人策略存在精度低、速度慢、对扰动敏感的问题。虽然可以通过强化学习改进，但真实世界训练成本高昂。仿真训练虽然便宜，但无约束的强化学习会利用接触和动力学不匹配，导致不安全且无法转移到硬件的策略。

Method: 提出SCORE框架，约束仿真中的强化学习到预训练生成策略的支持域。通过流转向技术实现约束，限制SCORE只能产生基础策略能够产生的动作，确保可转移行为的同时最大化策略改进。该方法无需蒸馏、使用稀疏奖励、保持基础策略不变。

Result: 在八项真实世界灵巧多指机器人操作任务中，SCORE将平均成功率从37.8%提升至89.9%，而最佳基线方法为59.5%。相比基础策略，SCORE用少36.8%的步数达到成功。

Conclusion: 当策略优化被适当约束时，仿真可以显著改进现实世界操作策略，SCORE为真实-仿真-真实策略改进提供了新范式。

Abstract: Robots trained on real world data tend to be imprecise, slow, and brittle to perturbations. Improving these policies with reinforcement learning (RL) is an appealing alternative, but this process often requires expensive training in the real world. Performing policy improvement in simulation instead provides a far cheaper alternative, but unconstrained RL in simulation can exploit contact and dynamics mismatches, resulting in unsafe behaviors that do not transfer to hardware. Common forms of regularization can furthermore limit improvement by overconstraining to an imperfect behavior prior. In this work, we propose Support-Constrained Off-Domain REinforcement (SCORE), a real-to-sim-to-real framework that constrains RL in simulation to the support of a generative policy pretrained on real data. We instantiate this constraint through flow steering, restricting SCORE to actions the base policy can already produce, which ensures transferable behaviors while maximizing policy improvement. Improving a policy with SCORE requires minimal effort: it learns from sparse rewards, avoids distillation, and leaves the base policy untouched. Across eight real-world dexterous multi-fingered robotic manipulation tasks, SCORE improves average success rate from 37.8% to 89.9%, compared to 59.5% for the best baseline, and reaches success in 36.8% fewer steps than the base policy. Ultimately, through extensive experiments and ablations, we show that simulation can substantially improve real-world manipulation policies when policy optimization is appropriately constrained, introducing a new paradigm for real-to-sim-to-real policy improvement. Videos and code are available at https://weirdlabuw.github.io/score/.

</details>
